\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01178}01178\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01179}01179\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ defines\ a\ matcher\ with\ the\ given\ name\ that\ executes\ the\ statements,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01180}01180\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ which\ must\ return\ a\ bool\ to\ indicate\ if\ the\ match\ succeeds.\ \ Inside}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01182}01182\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ refer\ to\ its\ type\ by\ 'arg\_type'.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01184}01184\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ description\ string\ documents\ what\ the\ matcher\ does,\ and\ is\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01185}01185\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ generate\ the\ failure\ message\ when\ the\ match\ fails.\ \ Since\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01186}01186\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ MATCHER()\ is\ usually\ defined\ in\ a\ header\ file\ shared\ by\ multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01187}01187\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ C++\ source\ files,\ we\ require\ the\ description\ to\ be\ a\ C-\/string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01188}01188\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ literal\ to\ avoid\ possible\ side\ effects.\ \ It\ can\ be\ empty,\ in\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01189}01189\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ case\ we'll\ use\ the\ sequence\ of\ words\ in\ the\ matcher\ name\ as\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01190}01190\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ description.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01191}01191\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01217}01217\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01218}01218\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ that\ the\ type\ of\ the\ value\ being\ matched\ (arg\_type)\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01219}01219\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ determined\ by\ the\ context\ in\ which\ you\ use\ the\ matcher\ and\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01220}01220\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ supplied\ to\ you\ by\ the\ compiler,\ so\ you\ don't\ need\ to\ worry\ about}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01221}01221\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ declaring\ it\ (nor\ can\ you).\ \ This\ allows\ the\ matcher\ to\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01222}01222\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ polymorphic.\ \ For\ example,\ IsEven()\ can\ be\ used\ to\ match\ any\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01223}01223\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ where\ the\ value\ of\ "{}(arg\ \%\ 2)\ ==\ 0"{}\ can\ be\ implicitly\ converted\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01224}01224\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ a\ bool.\ \ In\ the\ "{}Bar(IsEven())"{}\ example\ above,\ if\ method\ Bar()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{gmock-generated-matchers_8h_source_l01225}01225\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ takes\ an\ int,\ 'arg\_type'\ will\ be\ int;\ if\ it\ takes\ an\ unsigned\ long,}}
